 susheel koirala apane raajnneetik kariyar main haalanki ab tak kisi pad par nahin rahe
 Koirala, a devoted member of the Nepali Congress, has also served a three-year prison sentence in India for his involvement in the plane hijackings scandal in 1974
 is dauraan unhen tihaad sahit arriya, purniya or bhagalpur jelon main rakhaa gaya
 Koirala moved from Nepal to Kolkata in 1960 after the late Maharaj Mahendra of Nepal implemented a party-less panchayat system and imprisoned several leaders fighting for democracy
 kolkata main unhone pashchim bengal ke tatkaaleen mukhyamantri bidham chandra roy se mulaakaat kar nepal main loktantr ke liye chal rahe sangharsh par naitik samarthan maanga
 Koirala met several Indian leaders including Jayaprakash Narayan, Ram Manohar Lohia, Ashok Mehta and Madhu Dandavate on the issue and apprised them of Nepal's political situation and sought moral support from Indian political parties
 nirvaasan kaa jivan bitaate hue koirala ne nepali congress ke aadhikarik patr 'tarun' kaa sampadan kiya
 Koirala has been a member of the Central Executive of the Nepali Congress since 1979, and was elected general secretary in 1996 and vice president in 1998
 koirala ko 2008 main tatkaaleen adhyaksh girija prasad koirala dwaara nepali congress kaa kaaryakari adhyaksh niyukt kiya gaya, tathaa 2010 main vah party ke adhyaksh chun liye gaye
 All the 6 DMK ministers in the central government will submit their resignations on Monday
 diemke ko congress manaane kii koshish kar rahi he lekin sulah kii khabar ab tak nahin ai he
 However, the DMK has said that the Congress has not yet contacted him
 maamla tamilnadu main vidhansabha chunaavon main siton ke bantwaare kaa he
 Brajreshwari Shaktipeeth of Kangra is the miraculous abode of mother
 52 shaktipeethon main se ek brajareshwari shaktipeeth main sati kaa dahinaa vaksh gira tha
 Here 3 pindis of mother are worshiped as a symbol of 3 religions
 kehete hai jab maa sati ne pita ke dwaara kiye gaye shiv ke apmaan se kupit hokar apane pita raja daksh ke yajna kunda main kudakar apane praan tyaag die the tab krodhit shiv unki deh ko lekar puri sristi main ghume
 To calm Shiva's wrath, Lord Vishnu cut Mata Sati's body into pieces with her chakra
 sharir ke ye tukade dharti par jahaan-jahaan gire wo sthaan shaktipeeth kahalaaya
 It is believed that the right breast of the mother Sati fell here, so the mother's chest is worshiped in Brajreshwari Shaktipeeth
 mata brajareshwari kii ye shaktipeeth apane aap main anuthi or vishesh he kyonki yahaan maatr hindu bhakt hi sheesh nahin jhukaate balki muslim or sikh dharm ke shraddhalu bhi is dham main aakar apni aasthaa ke phool chadhaate hai
 It is said that the 3 domes of the Bajreshwari Devi temple are the symbol of these 3 religions, the first is a symbol of Hinduism, which has a temple-like shape, the second is a symbol of Muslim society and the third is the symbol of the Sikh sect
 3 gumbad vaale or 3 sampradaayon kii aasthaa kaa centre kahe jane vaale mata ke is dham main maa kii pindian bhi 3 teen hi hai
 This first and main pindi, reputed in the sanctum sanctorum of the temple, is that of Mother Brajreshwari
 duusari maa bhadrakaali or teesri or sabase choti pindi maa ekadshi kii he
 It was in this Shaktipeeth of Mother that his supreme devotee Dhyanu offered his head
 isiliye maa ke wo bhakt jo dhyanu ke anuyaayi bhi hai wo pile rang ke vastra dhaaran kar mandir main aate hai or maa kaa darshan pujan kar swayan ko dhanya karte hai
 It is said that any devotee who reaches the court of the mother with true devotion in his mind, his wishes are not complete
 phir chaahe manachaahe jeevanasathi kii kaamana ho yaa phir santan prapti kii chaah
 Mother fulfills the wishes of her every devotee
 maa ke is darbar main 5 baar aarti kaa vidhaan he jiskaa gavaah banane kii khwaahish har bhakt ke man main hoti he
 As soon as the gates of the temple open, devotees become anxious to worship the mother
 wo puja jisase puri hoti he unki har manokamana or hota he samast kashton kaa nivaaran
 In this Shaktipeeth of Mother Brajeshwari Devi, Aarti of Mother is done 5 times daily
 subah mandir ke kapaat khulte hi sabase pehle maa kii shaiyya ko uthaaya jaataa he
 After that, Mangala Aarti of the mother is done in the night makeup
 mangala aarti ke baad maa kaa raatri shringaar utaar kar unki teenon pindion kaa jal, doodh, dahi, ghi, or shahad ke panchamrita se abhishek kiya jaataa he
 After that, the mother is adorned with yellow sandal and she is dressed in new clothes and gold jewelery
 phir chanaa puri,fal or mewa kaa bhoga lagaakar maa kii praat: aarti sampann hoti he
 The mid-day aarti and the ritual of offering food are kept secret
 dopaher kii aarti ke liye mandir ke kapaat band rahete hai tab shraddhalu mandir parisar main hi bane ek vishesh sthaan par apane bacchon kaa mundan karavaate hai
 It is believed that by getting the children shaved here, the mother takes away all the disasters of the children's life
 mandir parisar main hi bhagwaan bhairav kaa bhi mandir he lekin is mandir main mahilaon kaa janaa purna rup se varjit hai
 The idol of Viraje Lord Bhairav is very special here
 Whenever there is any trouble on Kangra, then the tears of this idol and the body starts to sweat
 tab mandir ke pujari vishaal havan kaa aayojan kar maa se aane vaali aapadaa ko taalane kaa nivedan karte hai or ye brajeshwari shaktipeeth kaa chamatkaar or mahima hi he aane vaali har aapadaa maa ke ashish se tal jaati he
 In the afternoon, the doors of the temple are again opened to the devotees and the devotees arrive to seek the blessings of the mother
 kehete hai ekadshi ke din chaaval kaa prayog nahin kiya jaataa he lekin is shaktipeeth main maa ekadshi swayan maujuud he isliye yahaan bhoga main chaaval hi chadhaaya jaataa he
 After sunset, these pindi are bathed and anointed with Panchamrit again
 laal chandan, phool va nae vastra pahanaakar maa kaa shringaar kiya jaataa he or iske saath hi sampann hoti he sany kaal aarti
 The enjoyment of the evening aarti is distributed among the devotees in prasad form
 raat main samay aata he maa kii shayan aarti kaa, jab mandir ke pujari maa kii shaiyya taiyaar kar maa kii puja archana karte hai
 In Delhi's Sangam Vihar area, a young man was overwhelmed by flashing his pistol in front of friends
 yuvak ne apni hi pistal se khud ko galati se goli maar lee
 Friends took him to the hospital, but he died despite many attempts to save him
 is bare main police ne bataaya ki unhen batra hospital se phone aayaa ki do log ek yuvak ko lekar aae hai jiske sir par goli lagi he
 On receiving the call, the police team reached Batra Hospital where they found a young man named Amit in an injured condition
 batra hospital ne turant amit ko ames trama centre ke liye refer kar diya
 When the police team reached the trauma center of AIIMS with the injured Amit, the doctors declared him dead
 police kii jaanch me pataa chalaa kii sangam vihaar kaa rahane vaala amit apane ghar se gandhi camp me rahane vaale bablu se milane gaya tha
 Bablu and Amit drank beer there
 iske baad amit, bablu ke saath apane ghar ke liye nikal padaa
 On the way, Amit stopped the bike outside Rajneesh's house
 rajnish jaise hi ghar se baahar aayaa, tabhi rajnish kii nazar amit ke pistal par padi
 Amit had placed the pistol inside the shirt
 pistal dekhte hi rajnish ne usase poocha ki ise kyon lekar gum rahe ho
 At this, Amit said that he has taken this for his own safety and by saying this, he took out the magazine of the pistol and kept the pistol on his head and said that there is nothing
 rajnish or bablu ne police ko bataaya kii is dauraan donon use rokna chaah rahe the lekin tab tak usne goli chalaa di or pistal ke andar kii ek goli sidhe uske sir main ja lagi
 After this, both Bablu and Rajneesh went to the hospital with Amit
 police ne is maamle main gaiyr iradatan hatya or armas act kaa cese darj kiya he or jaanch kar rahi he
 Police is investigating Bablu's and Rajneesh's statements
 haal hi main pesh hue centre sarkaar ke tisare bajet kii kai yojanaon ke naamon main ahm badlaav kiye gaye hai
 In the budget, the government has changed the names of four schemes running in the name of former Prime Minister Rajiv Gandhi
 ek april se lagu honge nae naamkendre sarkaar ne inyojanaon ke naamon ko badalakampane kisi netaa yaa pasandida shakhsiyat kaa naam nahin rakhaa he
 The names of these schemes have been tried to look more politically neutral
 panchayat raaj mantralay ke antargat chalane vaali rajeev gandhi panchayat shashaktikaran yojana ke naam ko badalakar ab panchayat shashaktikaran yojana rakhaa gaya he

 viklang chaatro ko di jane vaali fellowship kaa nayaa naam rashtriya fellowship for students vid disabilities hoga

 upie shasankaal main shuru hui 'rajeev gandhi khel abhiyaan' ko sarkaar ne is bajet main khelo india yojana ke saath mila diya he

 pehle bhi badale gaye hai namisase pehle bhi centre sarkaar ne rajeev gandhi ke naam se chal rahi kai yojanaon kaa naam badla tha
 For example, the 'rajiv Gandhi Loan Scheme' designed to solve the housing problem of the weaker income citizens has been renamed as Pradhan Mantri Awas Yojana

 com / avuzeysqjm Navratri is celebrated four times a year, twice as secret Navaratri and twice as usual Navratri
 isamen caitra or asina navaratri zyada prasidd he
 Apart from this, Gupta Navratri is also celebrated in Magh and Ashada
 gupt navaratri, gopneey saadhnaaon ke liye zyada mahatvapurn maani jaati he
 In this, power is obtained and a boon is sought to destroy obstacles
 vaigyanik rup se is samay rituon main badlaav hota he or sharir main pitt kii maatra bad jaati he
 Therefore, if fasting or taking care of food is taken at this time, the person remains healthy
 is baar asadha maheene kii gupt navaratri 13 july se 21 july tak rahegi
 Make this amazing coincidence after 21 years, on Amavasya, do these measures in normal and Gupta Navaratri- In normal Navratri both sattvic and tantric worship is done
 - gupt navaratri main zyaadaatar tantric puja kii jaati he
 - In Gupta Navaratri, usually there is not much publicity, its practice is kept confidential
 - gupt navaratri main puja or manokamana jitani zyada gopneey hogi, safalataa utani hi zyada milegi
 What will be the method of worshiping the mother in Gupta Navaratri? - Kalash can be established for nine days
 - agar kalash kii sthapana kii he to donon vela mantra jaap,
 Chalisa or Saptashati should be recited
 - donon hi samay aarti bhi karnaa acha hoga
 - Offer both the Vela bhoga to the mother, the simplest and best enjoyment is cloves and betasha
 - maa ke liye laal phool sarvottam hota he par maa ko aak, madar, doob or tulsi bilkul na chadhayen 
 Keep your food and diet Satvik for the entire nine days
 masik shivaratri par raashi anusaar karen shiv pujashighra rojgaar kii prapti ke liye- devi ke samaksh ghi kaa deepak jalaaen
 - Take nine batches and put two cloves on each batche
 - ab saare bataashe ek-ek karke devi ko arpit karen
 - Use this on any night of Navratri
 sheeghra vivaah ke liye- devi ke samaksh roj ek ghi kaa deepak jalaaen
 After this, offer them a garland of red flowers every day
 - sheeghra vivaah kii prarthana karen
 - Use this every night of Navratri
 punjab ko sirf nashe kaa nasha nahin he
 With its Range Rover, s Class Mercedes, DJ music, dollars and broken English, he is addicted to everything that has nothing to do with Punjabi
 udata punjab ke har seen main punjab kam dikhataa he
 The film introduces the language culture of Punjab which is not even hybrid
 mishran kii jagah aaayaatit he
 In common parlance, abuses are accepted as if they were poetry of Surjeet Patar and Pash

 - bihar ke kuch zilon ke naam to 1997 se hi pichde zilon kii suchi main chale aa rahe hai
